## FAQ
How is Jeeva different from traditional sales tools?
Traditional tools track tasks, Jeeva does them. While most platforms require reps to manage dashboards, sequences, and CRMs manually, Jeeva acts like a proactive, agentic AI teammate. It doesn’t need micromanagement. It finds leads, sends outreach, follows up, and even handles objections — so your team can focus on closing, not clicking. 
Do I need a sales team to use Jeeva?
How much management does Jeeva need?
What kind of results can I expect?
Can Jeeva work with our existing tools and CRM?
Is there a minimum commitment to get started?

## Ok, here's what we do. Plain talk.
### What is Keyplay?
Keyplay is the account scoring and intelligence solution for modern GTM teams.
**Goal:** Work the right accounts.
Working as a companion to your CRM, Keyplay uses AI agents, fit signals, and intent signals to model your ideal customer, score & segment accounts, and surface new opportunities. It helps you prioritize best-fit accounts and understand your target market.
### What are the main use cases for Keyplay?
Keyplay helps marketing and sales prioritize and organize accounts for:
  * Territory Planning.
  * Account-Based Marketing & Advertising.
  * Outbound Enablement.
  * Inbound Lead Qualification.
  * Market Segmentation.


Keyplay is often purchased as part of a strategic initiative like:
  * Launching or revising an ABM strategy.
  * Expanding a sales-led motion (hiring more AEs and SDRs).
  * Optimizing or expanding a LinkedIn Ads strategy.
  * Entering new segments and/or moving up-market.
  * Launching new products or markets with distinct ICPs.


### What is an ICP model? How does it work in Keyplay?
99% of B2B companies want to focus on their true ICP. But the traditional "filter and flood" list building tools don't support a nuanced and dynamic ICP program.
There's a better way, an **ICP Model**.
An ICP Model uses account fit insights to represent your ideal customer profile with data. It helps you identify & prioritize your best-fit accounts with scoring, tiering, and intelligence.
It’s not just about company size or industry; it includes nuanced factors about each company’s business situation, activities, and problems, represented in signals or AI-driven insights. It’s a dynamic system that continuously ranks accounts for marketing and sales.
### What is "whitebox" intent? How does it work in Keyplay?
Whitebox intent means you can see exactly what drives each intent score – no more "voodoo magic" black box algorithms from legacy ABM platforms.
With Keyplay, you connect multiple intent sources (LinkedIn Ads engagement, website visits, custom signals from Clay/Zapier) through our simple API. We aggregate all these signals and show you which activities contributed to each account's intent score.
You control the scoring. Adjust how much weight each signal carries, test different models, and see results instantly. And since intent is layered on top of ICP fit scoring, you're only tracking intent for accounts that actually match your ideal customer profile – not wasting time on bad-fit accounts that happened to visit your website.
It's intent scoring that's transparent, flexible, and actually makes sense to your team.
### Who is Keyplay best for?
Keyplay is ideal for growing B2B SaaS & AI companies with a sales-led motion, 5+ AEs, and Salesforce or HubSpot CRM. We tend to work with companies from Series A to post-IPO.  
We are best for companies who
  1. Sell into complex, diverse markets (multiple verticals and segments).
  2. Have relatively wide TAMs (e.g. not just F500)
  3. Need to prioritize accounts for multiple segments
  4. Invest in account-based advertising (on LinkedIn and other places)
  5. Have a direct sales motion.


### How much does it cost?
You can use our platform & data, or you can engage with us more deeply as a service provider. We have two base packages:
Our **Growth plan is $18K/year** for ICP modeling with all standard fit signals, AI Lookalikes, CRM integrations, and ongoing scoring & enrichment for up to 75K CRM records. You can add-on credits for AI Agents.
Our **Full-Service ICP plans start at $29K/year** and increase based on customization, CRM account volume, and number of models. It includes everything in Growth, plus API access, multi-model support, intent scoring, and additional services.
### How does it integrate with my other tools?
Keyplay has a 2-way sync with Salesforce or HubSpot CRM, so you can operationalize your ICP within the systems you already use. CRM integrations work with OAuth connections (no managed package) and writes fields on the account record. You control the details.  
Keyplay also lets you sync account lists to Clay.  
For Intent scoring, we have native integrations with LinkedIn Ads, Snitcher, Phantombuster, and many more coming soon (in addition to our API to aggregate any custom intent signals).
### Can I get a free trial or proof of concept (POC)?
Yes, we offer proof of concept engagements to help you see how Keyplay works in your specific use case. It’s the easiest way to validate the impact before making a larger commitment.
Request a Demo to learn more about our POC process.
If you’re looking for a self-serve starter option, try our free List Builder plan.

## Engage, win, retain, repeat.
The all-in-one communication platform empowering revenue teams to act swiftly and personalize interactions at scale.
![Multi-line Power Dialer](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/ivr-icon.svg)
#### Multi-line Power Dialer
Dial up to 10 leads at a time while AI-Powered Machine Detection skips voicemails and [IVRs](https://www.kixie.com/features/ivr-auto-attendant/ "IVRs").
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/powerdialer/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/auto-sms-icon.svg)
#### Team SMS
Respond faster with [shared SMS](https://www.kixie.com/features/text-messaging/ "shared SMS") inboxes. Teams collaborate better and learn faster with internal notes.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/team-sms/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/local-presence-icon.svg)
#### Connection-Boost
AI-powered [local presence dialing](https://www.kixie.com/features/local-presence/ "local presence dialing") with progressive Caller ID and “Spam Risk” prevention built in.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/connectionboost/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/ai-icon.svg)
#### Conversation Intelligence
Track keywords, phrases, sentiment analysis, and more, with AI-generated call summaries synced to your CRM.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/conversation-intelligence/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/call-coaching-icon.svg)
#### Intelligent Call Routing
[Automatic call distribution](https://www.kixie.com/features/automatic-call-distribution/ "Automatic call distribution") (ACD) based on CRM fields connects callers to the right agent, hassle free.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/call-routing/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/call-disposition-icon.svg)
#### DNC List Compliance
No more manual list-checking. Help avoid penalties and ensure compliance without slowing down your team.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/national-dnc-compliance/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/byod-icon.svg)
#### Caller ID Reputation
Ensure your phone numbers represent your company’s best intentions. Avoid calls labeled “Spam Risk” to current and future customers.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/caller-id-reputation/)
![](https://kixie.com/assets/img/icon/data-icon.svg)
#### Realtime Reporting
Get instant feedback, foster friendly competition with [live leaderboards](https://www.kixie.com/features/live-leaderboards/), and analyze past data against current performance.
[Learn More ](https://www.kixie.com/features/live-leaderboards/)

THE FIERCEST COMPETITORS
###  Competitive   
Intelligence
Help your sellers work and win their competitive deals by delivering deal-based competitive insights directly into the tools they use every day.
[LEARN MORE ](https://klue.com/compete-agent)
###  Win-Loss
Capture and analyze objective feedback from your buyers to remove bias from decisions being made about your product and go-to-market strategy
[LEARN MORE ](https://klue.com/win-loss)
##  One   
platform
Klue brings together your competitive intelligence and win-loss programs into one place so you can enable your teams with the market, competitive, and buyer insights they need to win.
##  Deal-based competitive insights
Klue proactively supports sellers in all of their competitive deals by sending personalized, actionable content with recommendations on what they should do next. 
##  Win-Loss   
depth & quality
Klue’s team of experienced interviewers, analysts, and writers produce high-quality, more insightful interviews by extracting key insights on your competition, product, and more.
##  Integrated with your workplace
Deliver and retrieve competitive intel from the most important tools that your teams already use every single day.
[Learn More ](https://klue.com/product/integrations)

COMPETITIVE INTELLIGENCE AUTOMATION SOFTWARE 
# Win More Deals with Competitive Intelligence
Close even the most difficult of deals with always up-to-date Battlecards that live where your sales teams work.
**An hour a week is all you need** to track dozens of competitors and surface key, deal-winning insights. How? Put your competitive intelligence on autopilot and let AI filter out the noise.
Keep the **latest and greatest intel at the fingertips of your sales reps**. Updated Battlecards enable effective objection handling and an end to losing winnable deals.
**Increase competitive win rates** with Battlecards your sales team will actually use. Get automated win-loss reporting through integrations with the sales tools they work in every day.
![Kompyte+Semrush-CI-Advantage-V1](https://www.kompyte.com/hubfs/Logos%20Customers/Graphics%20and%20Illustrations%2023/Kompyte+Semrush-CI-Advantage-V1.svg)

## Real-time Competitive Intelligence at Scale
Kompyte automatically tracks your competitors’ updates across hundreds of sources and millions of data points.
Next, AI filters out the noise, surfacing actionable updates that might otherwise go unnoticed.
What used to take days now takes about an hour a week.
## Real-time Competitive Intelligence at Scale
Kompyte automatically tracks your competitors’ updates across hundreds of sources and millions of data points including:
  * Websites
  * Reviews
  * Content
  * Social
  * Ads
  * Job postings


Next, AI filters out the noise, surfacing actionable updates that might otherwise go unnoticed.
With [AI Daily Summaries](https://www.kompyte.com/kompyte-competitive-intelligence-automation-ai), what used to take days now takes about an hour a week.
![Kompyte-Conceptshots-Filters_Web-Tracking](https://www.kompyte.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Kompyte-Conceptshots-Filters_Web-Tracking.jpg?width=1304&height=815&name=Kompyte-Conceptshots-Filters_Web-Tracking.jpg)
![Kompyte-Conceptshots-Sharing-a-Battlecard](https://www.kompyte.com/hubfs/Kompyte-Conceptshots-Sharing-a-Battlecard.jpg)
## Battlecards Designed to Close More Deals
Sales-ready Battlecard templates curate key intelligence from any source. Adjust for the way your sales team closes deals by highlighting overviews, differentiators - anything!
Kompyte keeps your Battlecards consistent, up to date, and easily available. With bi-directional CRM and sales tool integrations, even new sales reps are equipped to close every winnable deal.
  * Surface competitive intelligence where your reps already work
  * Measure and increase the adoption of always-updated Battlecards and Reports

##  ![Kompyte-Conceptshots-Salesforc-battlecard-winrates](https://www.kompyte.com/hs-fs/hubfs/Conceptshots%2023/Kompyte-Conceptshots-Salesforc-battlecard-winrates.png?width=1162&height=814&name=Kompyte-Conceptshots-Salesforc-battlecard-winrates.png)Battlecards Your Sales Team will Actually Use
The best Battlecard is the one they’ll use.
That’s why we built bi-directional integrations with the CRMs and tools your sales team uses every day.
  * Measure and increase the adoption of always-updated battlecards and reports
  * Surface the direct impact of your competitive initiatives on revenue with automated win/loss calculations
  * Improve sales training, enabling new reps to sell faster.


## Deep Insights for Truly Informed Decisions
Win/loss analysis tools power your competitive intelligence program with real data such as competitive revenue, competitor frequency, and win rates - with and without battlecards. 
Through our research partner IcebergIQ, Kompyte becomes the single source of truth for all win/loss and churn/renewal insights. Put unbiased market feedback into action by populating Reports and Battlecards with key interview takeaways.
  * Surface the direct impact of your competitive initiatives on revenue with automated win/loss calculations
  * Quantitative and qualitative data provide a 360-degree view of the market
  * Candid customer feedback completes the picture

# Not all platforms are built the same
### Koncert is the only ultra-low latency AI dialer platform in the industry
[Learn More](https://www.koncert.com/why-koncert)
  

### The B2B sales tools you need to power up more conversations and pipeline
Koncert’s AI Dialer platform intelligently filtersthrough voicemails and phone trees and connect live calls.Caller IDs are kept clean and managed for you. Local Caller IDs are automatically selected based on prospect’s area code. Enjoy lightning-fast connects, have more conversations and effortlessly achieve your sales goals.

###### Quick Connect
Phone tech and AI are embedded in one network, delivering ultra-low latency connects, giving you a fighting change to set meetings when calls are connected.
###### Automated Local Presence
Local Caller IDs are automatically selected based on prospect’s area code, delivering true local presence and better connect rates.
###### Automated Caller ID Health
Heat Map monitors daily usage. We scan Caller IDs’ appearance in real mobile phones. Caller IDs are kept clean and managed for you, to ensure bad Spam numbers are cleaned or removed so your best prospect isn’t avoiding your call.
###### Analytics
Easily drill down to see performance at a rep level or list level. Helps to quickly identify issues and opportunities to improve team performance.

###### Remote Coach
Sales coaching done at scale. Managers can surf through live calls or listen to call recordings. During live calls, managers can coach the rep in real time, without the prospect hearing.
###### Remote Salesfloor
Virtual Salesfloor for a call blitz or a ride-along as if you were in the office. Reps gain motivation and learn from each other. More togetherness helps improve adoption and effectiveness.
###### Conversation Intelligence
AI scans and detects objections, allowing managers to coach the reps, at scale. Store specific calls in a call library, allowing reps learn from examples.
###### Parking Lot
Parking Lot quarantines bad numbers using workflow rules so your team can focus on the legit ones. Reps are not wasting dials calling the same “bad numbers”.

## Personas & Use Cases
####  Tools for every sales role to get the job done with ease
#### Account Executives
Click to flip
Cover 100% of your ideal customers in your target market with phone conversations along with emails. Prospecting made easy. You can keep adding new opportunities steadilyand keep the pipeline humming.
#### XDR Managers
Click to flip
Dashboards and call recordings help you to train and coach your SDRs/BDRs/TDRs. See how well they are covering their accounts.
#### Chief Revenue Officers
Click to flip
Empower your sales team to continuously find new opportunities. Shorten sales cycles. Get more revenue.
#### Inside & Field Sales Managers
Click to flip
Increase your sales team’s productivity. Track the number of dials made, emails sent, call connects, and conversations. Coach and collaborate with your team.
#### Marketing
Click to flip
Improve MQL to SQL conversion ratio through more conversations. Track follow-ups to webinars, inbound leads, and marketing campaigns.
#### Inbound
Click to flip
Improve speed to lead. Empower reps to connect with inbound leads quickly and often. Increase the conversion ratio.
#### Outbound
Click to flip
Power up more conversations through phone calls at scale. Effortlessly complete longer list of call tasks and cut the back log in a sequencer. 
#### Account-Based Sales
Click to flip
Empower reps to identify many personas in target accounts and connect with them easily. Multi-threading in each target account increasesthe chances of closing more opportunities.

The Problem
## Everyone is using the same database. That's the problem.
Apollo, ZoomInfo, Lusha — they all pull from the same sources.
Your competitors are sending the exact same emails to the exact same people.
When everyone has the same data, nobody has an edge.
A data edge is data your competitors don't have — custom to your business, built from live sources, refreshed continuously, structured for execution.
The teams winning today don't rent databases. They build their own.
How your data edge gets built

How It Works
## Describe what you need. Kuration builds it.
Step 1
### Tell us what you need
In plain English.
"Find all exhibitors from CES 2025 with VP+ contacts in EMEA."
No workflows. No filters. Just a sentence.
Step 2
### AI agents research for you
Kuration searches, extracts, cross-checks, and enriches from live sources — websites, PDFs, directories, events, maps, registries.
Sources active:

Extracting & enriching...
Step 3
### Get a ready-to-use list
Verified companies, decision-maker contacts, custom attributes. Export to CSV, Sheets, or your CRM.

Popular

Out:Business list + owner contacts + reviews + details
Extract businesses from Google Maps by category and location. Get owner contacts, ratings, and business details.

The cookies that are categorized as "Necessary" are stored on your browser as they are essential for enabling the basic functionalities of the site. ... Show more
NecessaryAlways Active
Necessary cookies are required to enable the basic features of this site, such as providing secure log-in or adjusting your consent preferences. These cookies do not store any personally identifiable data.
  * Cookie
__cf_bm
  * Duration
1 hour
  * Description
This cookie, set by Cloudflare, is used to support Cloudflare Bot Management. 


  * Cookie
wt_consent
  * Duration
1 year
  * Description
Used for remembering users’ consent preferences to be respected on subsequent site visits. It does not collect or store personal information about visitors to the site.


  * Cookie
_cfuvid
  * Duration
session
  * Description
Calendly sets this cookie to track users across sessions to optimize user experience by maintaining session consistency and providing personalized services


  * Cookie
__hssrc
  * Duration
session
  * Description
This cookie is set by Hubspot whenever it changes the session cookie. The __hssrc cookie set to 1 indicates that the user has restarted the browser, and if the cookie does not exist, it is assumed to be a new session.


  * Cookie
__hssc
  * Duration
1 hour
  * Description
HubSpot sets this cookie to keep track of sessions and to determine if HubSpot should increment the session number and timestamps in the __hstc cookie.


  * Cookie
AWSALBCORS
  * Duration
7 days
  * Description
Amazon Web Services set this cookie for load balancing.


  * Cookie
PHPSESSID
  * Duration
session
  * Description
This cookie is native to PHP applications. The cookie stores and identifies a user's unique session ID to manage user sessions on the website. The cookie is a session cookie and will be deleted when all the browser windows are closed.


Functional
Functional cookies help perform certain functionalities like sharing the content of the website on social media platforms, collecting feedback, and other third-party features.
  * Cookie
__zlcmid
  * Duration
1 year
  * Description
Zopim sets this cookie to store a unique user ID.


  * Cookie
zte*
  * Duration
session
  * Description
Zendesk sets this cookie to ensure the proper functionality of the chat widget by identifying the domain or subdomain where the chat feature is used.


Analytics
Analytical cookies are used to understand how visitors interact with the website. These cookies help provide information on metrics such as the number of visitors, bounce rate, traffic source, etc.
  * Cookie
__hstc
  * Duration
6 months
  * Description
Hubspot set this main cookie for tracking visitors. It contains the domain, initial timestamp (first visit), last timestamp (last visit), current timestamp (this visit), and session number (increments for each subsequent session).


  * Cookie
hubspotutk
  * Duration
6 months
  * Description
HubSpot sets this cookie to keep track of the visitors to the website. This cookie is passed to HubSpot on form submission and used when deduplicating contacts.


  * Cookie
_ga
  * Duration
1 year 1 month 4 days
  * Description
Google Analytics sets this cookie to calculate visitor, session and campaign data and track site usage for the site's analytics report. The cookie stores information anonymously and assigns a randomly generated number to recognise unique visitors.


  * Cookie
_ga_*
  * Duration
1 year 1 month 4 days
  * Description
Google Analytics sets this cookie to store and count page views.


Performance
Performance cookies are used to understand and analyze the key performance indexes of the website which helps in delivering a better user experience for the visitors.
No cookies to display.

## All-in-One B2B Lead Intelligence Platform
**Lead411** is a powerful _B2B lead generation database and sales intelligence platform_ that helps sales teams, marketers, and business development professionals reach the right decision-makers faster. With **real-time verified contact data** , growth intent signals, and seamless CRM integrations, Lead411 makes it easy to build pipelines, close deals, and scale outreach efforts efficiently.
### What Lead411 Offers:
  * **[B2B Lead Generation](https://www.lead411.com/data-solutions/lead-prospecting/):** Access millions of verified emails, direct dials, and company profiles to fuel your outreach strategy.
  * **[Sales Intelligence Alerts](https://www.lead411.com/data-solutions/lead-scoring/):** Stay ahead of the competition with real-time notifications for hiring, funding, executive changes, and company growth signals.
  * **[Growth Intent Data](https://www.lead411.com/data-solutions/bombora-intent-data/):** Pinpoint companies that are actively growing or in buying mode using behavioral indicators and industry-specific trends.
  * **[Sales Intelligence API](https://www.lead411.com/pricing/):** Seamlessly connect the best sales lead database into your platform, CRM, or application with our developer-friendly API.
  * **[Unlimited Search Plans](https://www.lead411.com/pricing/):** Unlike other providers, Lead411 offers _truly unlimited search and export capabilities_ on select plans—no daily caps or usage limits.
  * **[CRM& Outreach Integration](https://www.lead411.com/data-solutions/crm-enhancer/):** Sync directly with Salesforce, HubSpot, Outreach.io, and more for frictionless prospecting and lead management.
  * **[Advanced Search Filters](https://www.lead411.com/data-solutions/lead-prospecting/):** Drill down by industry, company size, technologies used, location, job title, and more—get hyper-targeted results in seconds.


### Why Choose Lead411?
Thousands of companies—from fast-growing startups to Fortune 500 teams—use Lead411 to **accelerate revenue growth** , **shorten sales cycles** , and **boost outbound performance**. Whether you’re looking for _accurate b2b contact data provider_ or _intent-driven targeting_ , Lead411 delivers the insights you need to win more deals.

## Lead411 Frequently Asked Questions
What is Lead411?
Lead411 is a B2B sales intelligence platform that provides real-time verified contact data, growth intent signals, trigger alerts and b2b sales leads to help businesses identify and reach decision-makers quickly.
How does Lead411 verify contact information?
Lead411 uses a combination of machine learning, human verification, and real-time email validation to ensure all contact data is accurate and up to date.
What kind of data does Lead411 provide?
Lead411 provides email addresses, direct dial phone numbers, company insights, job titles, technologies used, hiring trends, and intent signals for B2B prospects.
What industries does Lead411 serve?
Lead411 serves a wide range of industries including SaaS, IT services, manufacturing, healthcare, marketing agencies, and financial services.
Does Lead411 offer a free trial?
Yes, Lead411 offers a free trial that includes 50 free leads so you can test the platform and explore its features before committing.
Is Lead411 better than ZoomInfo or Apollo?
Lead411 offers more affordable pricing, unlimited b2b leads on select plans, real-time verified data, and better contract flexibility compared to ZoomInfo and Apollo.
Does Lead411 offer an API like Apollo?
Lead411 offers an unlimited b2b data api that is much less expensive than [Apollo API Pricing](https://www.lead411.com/blog/apollo-io-api-pricing/).
Can I integrate Lead411 with my CRM?
Yes, Lead411 integrates with popular CRMs such as Salesforce, HubSpot, Pipedrive, and others, enabling seamless data sync and automation.
What is growth intent data on Lead411?
Growth intent data shows which companies are expanding, hiring, or investing—giving you buying signals to prioritize outreach at the right time.
Does Lead411 support team accounts?
Yes, Lead411 supports multiple users and team accounts, making it ideal for sales teams, marketing departments, and agencies.
How often is the data updated on Lead411?
Lead411 updates its contact database continuously, with millions of contact points validated in real-time using AI and manual checks.
Is there a daily or monthly download limit?
No, Lead411 offers unlimited lead searches and exports on most plans, unlike competitors that limit daily usage.
Can I cancel my Lead411 subscription anytime?
Yes, Lead411 is known for its flexible contract terms. You can cancel or adjust your plan without long-term lock-ins, unlike many other providers.
How accurate is Lead411’s phone number and email data?
Lead411 offers 96%+ accuracy on email deliverability and provides direct-dial phone numbers verified through multi-layer validation methods.
Does Lead411 offer intent integrations like Bombora?
Yes, Lead411 offers native intent data but also integrates with Bombora and other third-party intent platforms depending on your plan.
How do I get started with Lead411?
You can sign up on Lead411.com for a free trial with 50 leads. After that, choose a plan that fits your team size and data needs.

## Features
Everything you need to find and contact property owners
Our AI-powered skip-tracing platform is designed specifically for real estate professionals who need accurate contact information fast.
    
Our AI algorithms deliver industry-leading 95% match rates for property owner contact information.
    
Access billions of records from multiple sources including public records, consumer data, and proprietary datasets.
    
Ask questions about your data in plain English and get instant insights with our AI-powered chat interface.
    
Stay compliant with TCPA, FCRA, and other regulations with our built-in compliance tools and documentation.
    
Gain insights into your leads with property valuation, ownership history, and demographic information.
    
Process thousands of records in seconds, not days, with our high-performance cloud infrastructure.
    
Export your enriched data in multiple formats including CSV, Excel, and direct CRM integrations.
    
Automatically clean and standardize your data with our AI-powered data cleaning tools.
## How It Works
Four simple steps to find property owners
Our streamlined process makes it easy to go from a list of properties to actionable contact information in minutes.
![Upload your list](https://www.leadenrich.com/file-upload-desk.png)
01Step 01
### Upload your list
Upload your property list in CSV, Excel, or text format. We accept addresses, owner names, or any combination of data you have.
![AI processes your data](https://www.leadenrich.com/interconnected-insights.png)
02Step 02
### AI processes your data
Our AI algorithms search billions of records across multiple databases to find the most accurate and up-to-date contact information.
![Review and clean results](https://www.leadenrich.com/data-review-session.png)
03Step 03
### Review and clean results
Review your results in our interactive dashboard. Use our AI chat to ask questions about your data and our cleaning tools to standardize formats.
![Export and take action](https://www.leadenrich.com/placeholder.svg?height=300&width=400&query=real%20estate%20agent%20making%20phone%20call)
04Step 04
### Export and take action
Export your enriched data to CSV, Excel, or directly to your CRM. Start contacting property owners and closing more deals.

## Universal Identity Architecture
### Transforming raw signals into a precise framework for every individual.
Our engine creates universal structured data pipelines from billions of unstructured signals. By ingesting raw data from diverse sources, we forge an ever-evolving identity graph that adapts in real-time. 
We connect the dots between **B2B and B2C identities** , bridging the gap between personal and work devices. Our graph synthesizes **online and offline actions** into a single, unified profile—giving you the totality of a person, not just a fragment. 
  * B2B & B2C Bridging
  * Cross-Device Identity
  * Behavioral Resolution

FAQs
# frequently asked questions
### What is Precision Data?
Precision Data is highly specific and verified datasets tailored to a business’s unique needs, rather than generic, one-size-fits-all records.
### How is LeadGenius different?
Unlike static databases, LeadGenius delivers on-demand data, AI + Human-in-the-Loop sourcing, and global coverage across hard-to-find segments—fully compliant with GDPR and CCPA.
### How much does LeadGenius cost?
Pricing depends on your needs and scale. Packages are tailored to business size and requirements. Contact LeadGenius for a detailed quote.
### How does LeadGenius use AI?
LeadGenius leverages AI and LLMs to process billions of resources, combined with Human-in-the-Loop checks for accuracy and strategic depth. The Tagger system also organizes insights and creates lookalike audiences.

# Contact-Level Technographics: The Future of Precision Audience Building
Traditional B2B databases stop at account-level installs—useful logos, but little insight into who actually drives adoption. Contact-Level Technographics (CLT) goes deeper by mapping real practitioner behavior from GitHub, Stack Overflow, and other public-web signals back to verified business identities.
[read more](https://www.leadgenius.com/resources/contact-level-technographics-the-future-of-precision-audience-building)

## Your Data Security, Our Priority

![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60819f9be381394642b5659e/68714db6de2a91f39ebb1a78_icon.svg)
SOC 2 Type II Compliant: Audited regularly to meet stringent security and privacy standards.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60819f9be381394642b5659e/68714db6de2a91f39ebb1a78_icon.svg)
GDPR-Ready: Global data protection compliance built-in.
![](https://cdn.prod.website-files.com/60819f9be381394642b5659e/68714db6de2a91f39ebb1a78_icon.svg)
Data Encryption: Comprehensive encryption both in transit and at rest.

Role-Based Access Control: Customize user permissions to safeguard your data.

The QUIC.cloud server hel229-hyb-worker.quic.cloud was not able to connect to the site's origin server.
2026-02-20 11:27:44 UTC
### Web Browser
### QUIC.cloud Node
### Origin Server
### Why did this happen?
This site is using [QUIC.cloud](https://www.quic.cloud/) CDN. This error indicates that our QUIC.cloud nodes were unable to reach the website’s origin server.
### If you're a visitor
Please try again later.
### If you're the website owner
Please verify that your **Connection Type to Origin** and **Server IP** are set correctly in the QUIC.cloud CDN Configuration.
See these additional [troubleshooting steps](https://docs.quic.cloud/troubleshooting/httperror/#520-origin-server-unavailable).
